<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verduistering.html>verduistering</a> (15105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verduisteren.html>verduisteren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verduistering.html>verduistering</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verduisteringen.html>verduisteringen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verduistering.html>verduisteringetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">verduisterinkje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>darkening</li>
<li>embezzlement</li>
<li>blackout; the mandatory blinding of all light emanating from <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a> to prevent bombing <a href = vnd.unilang:raids.html>raids</a> during the WW II occupation</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verdwinen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dwinen</i>. The base verb derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dwīnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dwīnaną</i>.
</p>

***vereiste.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vereiste.html>vereiste</a> (16604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vereisen.html>vereisen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to require</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.

***veren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veren.html>veren</a> (5849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vederen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vederijn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fetherīn</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veer.html>veer</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veren.html>veren</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>made of <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a>, plumose</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veren.html>veren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veer.html>veer</a></i></span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veer.html>veer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to the etymology above.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bounce, reverberate, spring.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:veren.html>veren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ferien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*farjaną</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verfilmen.html>verfilmen</a> (38758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:verfilmen.html>verfilmen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verfilmen.html>verfilmen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> of, to turn into a movie <span class="defdate">[from 1913]</span>
<ul><li><b>1913</b> March 14, "<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> zegetocht <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>", tr. from German, in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuws.html>nieuws</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> Nederlandsch-Indië</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>Vol</a>. 18, No. 61, folio 3, page 1; a <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> and redacted article from <i><a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>Das</a> Echo</i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eindelijk.html>eindelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> levensverrichtingen „<b><a href = vnd.unilang:verfilmd.html>verfilmd</a></b>” <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijft.html>blijft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gesproken.html>gesproken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woord.html>woord</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:niemendal.html>niemendal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>...</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">And finally all activities in life will be <b><a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> into <a href = vnd.unilang:films.html>films</a></b> and of language, of the <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> word, nothing at all will remain any more...</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>

***vergeetachtig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeetachtig.html>vergeetachtig</a> (32190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-achtig</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeetachtig.html>vergeetachtig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeetachtiger.html>vergeetachtiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vergeetachtigst</b>)

***vergen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergen.html>vergen</a> (20663)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergen.html>vergen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fergon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fergōną</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">fergon</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">fergje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fergen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">fergja</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ask, inquire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to offer, grant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to taunt, bother</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seek, search</li></ol>

***vergeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a> (428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vergēten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fargetan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*fragetan</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to forget <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">lose remembrance of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ve <b><a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></b> his name.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to forget <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fail to do</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vergat.html>vergat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b><a href = vnd.unilang:forgot.html>forgot</a></b> to lock the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to leave <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fail to take</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sleutel.html>sleutel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ve <b>left</b> my key at home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> tenses of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></i> are predominantly construed with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i> for all senses, but the construction with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> equally common in the sense “fail to take”. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also somewhat common in the sense “fail to do”, but quite <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> in the sense “lose memory of”.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">  past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geheugen.html>geheugen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verloren.html>verloren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:ver.html>ver</a> + <a href = vnd.unilang:gezocht.html>gezocht</a> past participle of <a href = vnd.unilang:zoeken.html>zoeken</a>. Used as in figurative speech, since it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not obvious to search far away of where you are.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergieten.html>vergieten</a> (24350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergieten.html>vergieten</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gieten.html>gieten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergieten.html>vergieten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spill, to shed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drain, to pour <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make liquid, to liquidise</li></ol>
